focus_tree = {
	id = GXC_focus_tree

	country = {
		factor = 0

		modifier = {
			add = 100
			tag = GXC
		}
	}

	default = no

	continuous_focus_position = { x = 4000 y = 2500 }

	shared_focus = UPC_the_road_to_unification

	#Coalition Focuses
	shared_focus = UPC_affairs_of_the_ruling_coalition

	shared_focus = UPC_calls_for_a_constitutional_convention

	#Foreign Policy Tree
	shared_focus = KMT_lead_the_liberation_of_asia
	shared_focus = CHN_return_to_the_world_stage_focus

##Political Tree
	focus = {
		id = GXC_twin_provinces_one_destiny
		icon = GFX_goal_SZC_recover_the_first_province
		cost = 4
		x = 13
		y = 1
		allow_branch = {
			GXC_is_phase_1_trigger = yes
		}
		ai_will_do = { base = 100 }
		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Focus Completed GXC_twin_provinces_one_destiny"
			add_command_power = 30
		}
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL }
	}

##Military Tree
	focus = {
		id = GXC_lessons_of_the_german_advisory_mission
		icon = GFX_goal_German_Staff
		cost = 4
		x = 33
		y = 2
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 100

			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				GXC_ai_factor_prioritize_military_focuses_trigger = yes
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				GXC_is_phase_1_trigger = yes #Helps them win the minigame
			}
		}
		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Focus Completed GXC_lessons_of_the_german_advisory_mission"
			if = {
				limit = { GXC_is_phase_1_trigger = yes }
				add_command_power = 25 #Helps win the minigame - equivalent to 1x cost to secure state + a 5 CP buffer.
			}
			army_experience = 25
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment amount = 750 producer = GEA }
			add_doctrine_cost_reduction = {
				cost_reduction = 0.50
				name = GXC_lessons_of_the_german_advisory_mission
				category = land_doctrine
			}
		}
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_ARMY_BONUS }
	}

	focus = {
		id = GXC_consolidate_the_regional_auxiliaries
		icon = GFX_goal_generic_officer
		cost = 4
		x = -3
		y = 1
		ai_will_do = { #increased weight for early Command Power Gain
			base = 200
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				GXC_ai_factor_prioritize_military_focuses_trigger = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				GXC_is_phase_1_trigger = yes #Helps them win the minigame
			}
		}
		relative_position_id = GXC_lessons_of_the_german_advisory_mission
		prerequisite = { focus = GXC_lessons_of_the_german_advisory_mission }
		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Focus Completed GXC_consolidate_the_regional_auxiliaries"
			if = {
				limit = { GXC_is_phase_1_trigger = yes }
				add_command_power = 50 #Helps win the minigame - equivalent of securing 2 states + 10 pt buffer.
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = support_equipment amount = 250 producer = GEA }
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = GXC_consolidate_the_regional_auxiliaries
				bonus = 0.5
				uses = 1
				category = support_tech
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			custom_effect_tooltip = GXC_consolidate_the_regional_auxiliaries_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				division_template = {
					name = "Lianhe Bubing"
					division_names_group = GXC_INF_01
					regiments = {
						irregular_infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
						irregular_infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
						irregular_infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
						irregular_infantry = { x = 0 y = 3 }
						irregular_infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
						irregular_infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
						irregular_infantry = { x = 1 y = 2 }
						irregular_infantry = { x = 1 y = 3 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_ARMY_BONUS }
	}

	focus = {
		id = GXC_insistence_upon_the_stiff_arm
		icon = GFX_goal_generic_police_state
		cost = 4
		x = -1
		y = 1
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				GXC_ai_factor_prioritize_military_focuses_trigger = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				GXC_is_phase_1_trigger = yes #Helps them win the minigame
			}
		}
		relative_position_id = GXC_consolidate_the_regional_auxiliaries
		prerequisite = { focus = GXC_consolidate_the_regional_auxiliaries }
		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetLogRoot]: Focus Completed GXC_insistence_upon_the_stiff_arm"
			if = {
				limit = { GXC_is_phase_1_trigger = yes }
				add_command_power = 100 #Helps win the minigame - equivalent to securing 4 states.
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_tech = tech_military_police }
				}
				set_technology = { tech_military_police = 1 }
			}
			else = {
				add_tech_bonus = {
					name = GXC_insistence_upon_the_stiff_arm
					bonus = 0.75
					uses = 1
					category = military_police_tech
				}
			}
			enable_tech_anti_partisan = yes
			add_stability = 0.05
			add_command_power = 15
		}
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_ARMY_BONUS }
	}

			hidden_effect = {
				country_lock_all_division_template = no
				if = {
					limit = { china_is_aligned_with_kmt = yes }
					country_event = { id = GXC.earlygame.001 days = 10 } #Fate of the Old Guangxi Clans
					country_event = { id = GXC.earlygame.003 days = 14 } #Fate of the Yue Army
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { china_is_aligned_with_federalists = yes }
					country_event = { id = GXC.earlygame.001 days = 10 } #Fate of the Old Guangxi Clans
					country_event = { id = GXC.earlygame.002 days = 14 } #Fate of the Kuomintang Remnants
				}
				else = {
					country_event = { id = GXC.earlygame.002 days = 10 } #Fate of the Kuomintang Remnants
					country_event = { id = GXC.earlygame.003 days = 14 } #Fate of the Yue Army
				}
			}
